import logging
import asyncio
import os
import sys
import multiprocessing as mp
import time
import json
import platform
import numpy as np
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional, Tuple, AsyncGenerator

# Since we are in EXECUTION and the user wants radical stability,
# we strictly avoid local imports that might fail until they are proven.
try:
    from .provider import LLMProvider
    from core.resilience.resource_arbitrator import get_resource_arbitrator
    from core.schemas import ChatStreamEvent
    from core.utils.concurrency import run_io_bound, RobustLock
except ImportError:
    # Minimal fallback interface if provider.py or schemas.py is missing/broken
    class LLMProvider:
        pass
    class ChatStreamEvent:
        def __init__(self, **k): self.__dict__.update(k)

logger = logging.getLogger("LLM.MLX")

class MLXLocalClient(LLMProvider):
    """
    Resilient MLX Client: Manages an isolated MLX worker process via ForkServer.
    ForkServer is safer for macOS ARM64 / Metal state inheritance.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, model_path: str, temp: float = 0.7, top_p: float = 0.9, max_tokens: int = 1024, device: str = "gpu"):
        self.model_path = model_path
        self.temp = temp
        self.top_p = top_p
        self.max_tokens = max_tokens
        self.device = device
        
        # Multiprocessing primitives
        try:
            # Forkserver is critical for macOS/Metal safety
            mp.set_start_method("forkserver", force=True)
        except RuntimeError as _e:
            logger.debug('Ignored RuntimeError in mlx_client.py: %s', _e)
            
        self._req_q = mp.Queue()
        self._res_q = mp.Queue()
        self._process: Optional[mp.Process] = None
        self._lock: Optional[RobustLock] = None
        self._init_done = False
        
        # [STEERING] Shared memory for affective substrate state (64 floats)
        self._substrate_mem = mp.Array('f', 64)
        self._sync_task: Optional[asyncio.Task] = None

    @property
    def lock(self) -> RobustLock:
        """Loop-aware robust lock for MLX worker management."""
        if self._lock is None:
            self._lock = RobustLock("MLX.WorkerLock")
        return self._lock

    @staticmethod
    def _drain_queue(q: mp.Queue):
        """Drain all stale messages from a multiprocessing queue."""
        drained = 0
        try:
            while not q.empty():
                q.get_nowait()
                drained += 1
        except Exception as _e:
            logger.debug('Ignored Exception in mlx_client.py: %s', _e)
        if drained:
            logger.debug("[MLX] Drained %d stale messages from queue.", drained)

    def _kill_stale_workers(self):
        """Kill ALL stale MLX ForkServer workers from previous Aura sessions.
        
        This is the permanent fix for MTLCompilerService exhaustion.
        Stale workers hold open Metal/GPU handles, preventing new workers from
        compiling shaders. On a 64GB Mac, stale workers can still exhaust Metal.
        """
        import subprocess
        try:
            # Find all forkserver processes that belong to our project
            result = subprocess.run(
                ["pgrep", "-f", "forkserver.*autonomy_engine"],
                capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=5
            )
            pids = [p.strip() for p in result.stdout.strip().split("\n") if p.strip()]
            
            if pids:
                logger.warning("🧹 [MLX] Found %d stale ForkServer workers. Cleaning up Metal handles...", len(pids))
                for pid in pids:
                    try:
                        os.kill(int(pid), 9)  # SIGKILL
                    except (ProcessLookupError, ValueError):
                        logger.debug('Ignored Exception in mlx_client.py: %s', "unknown_error")
                # Give OS time to reclaim Metal handles
                import time
                time.sleep(0.5)
                logger.info("✅ [MLX] Stale worker cleanup complete. Metal handles released.")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.debug("[MLX] Stale worker probe failed (non-fatal): %s", e)

    def _spawn_worker(self):
        """Spawns a fresh worker process using 'spawn' context.
        
        CRITICAL: We use mp.get_context('spawn') instead of the default 'forkserver'.
        The 'forkserver' method inherits the parent's Metal XPC connection to 
        MTLCompilerService, which becomes stale and causes generation failures.
        'spawn' creates a completely clean process with a fresh Metal context.
        """
        # Kill zombies before spawning to prevent Metal exhaustion
        self._kill_stale_workers()
        
        # [HOTSWAP] Enforce single heavy model lock
        _enforce_active_model_lock(self.model_path)
        
        try:
            from .mlx_worker import _mlx_worker_loop
        except ImportError:
            from core.brain.llm.mlx_worker import _mlx_worker_loop
        
        # Use spawn context for clean Metal XPC connection
        ctx = mp.get_context("spawn")
        
        # Recreate queues using spawn context for compatibility
        self._req_q = ctx.Queue()
        self._res_q = ctx.Queue()
        
        logger.info("🧠 [MLX] Spawning worker with model: %s", self.model_path)
        p = ctx.Process(
            target=_mlx_worker_loop,
            args=(self.model_path, self._req_q, self._res_q, self.device, self._substrate_mem),
            daemon=True,
            name=f"MLXWorker-{os.path.basename(self.model_path)}"
        )
        p.start()
        return p

    def __del__(self):
        """Ensure worker is killed when client is garbage collected."""
        try:
            if self._process and self._process.is_alive():
                self._process.kill()
                self._process.join(timeout=2.0)
        except Exception as _e:
            logger.debug('Ignored Exception in mlx_client.py: %s', _e)

    async def warm_up(self):
        """Pre-loads the model into RAM asynchronously so the first generation is instantaneous."""
        logger.info("🔥 [MLX] Pre-warming Local-MLX model into RAM...")
        try:
            await self._ensure_worker_alive()
            logger.info("✅ [MLX] Model is fully resident in RAM.")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning("⚠️ [MLX] Pre-warm failed, will retry on first prompt: %s", e)

    async def _ensure_worker_alive(self):
        """Self-healing supervisor for the MLX worker."""
        async with self.lock:
            # If process vanished or crashed, respawn
            if not self._process or not self._process.is_alive():
                # Drain any stale responses left by dead workers
                self._drain_queue(self._res_q)
                self._drain_queue(self._req_q)
                
                logger.info("📡 [MLX] Spawning isolated ForkServer worker...")
                self._process = self._spawn_worker()
                
                # Check for successful init in worker
                try:
                    # Initial load usually takes time, so we wait up to 300s for large models
                    # We use run_io_bound to avoid saturating the default thread pool
                    res = await asyncio.wait_for(run_io_bound(self._res_q.get), timeout=300.0)
                    if res.get("status") == "ok":
                        self._init_done = True
                        # Track if worker auto-downgraded to CPU
                        worker_device = res.get("device", self.device)
                        if worker_device == "cpu" and self.device != "cpu":
                            logger.warning("⚠️ [MLX] Worker auto-downgraded to CPU. Persisting for future respawns.")
                            self.device = "cpu"
                        logger.info("✅ [MLX] Worker ready and model loaded (device=%s).", self.device)
                    else:
                        err_msg = res.get("message", "Init failed")
                        if "RESOURCE_EXHAUSTED" in err_msg:
                            logger.warning("⚠️ [MLX] Metal exhausted during init. Switching to CPU for future spawns.")
                            self.device = "cpu"
                        raise RuntimeError(err_msg)
                except Exception as e:
                    import traceback
                    logger.error("❌ [MLX] Worker boot stalled/failed: %s", e)
                    traceback.print_exc()
                    # Safe version parsing
                    release_str = platform.mac_ver()[0]
                    v = release_str.split(".")
                    mac_ver = f"{v[0]}.{v[1]}" if len(v) >= 2 else v[0]
                    
                    os.environ["MACOSX_DEPLOYMENT_TARGET"] = mac_ver
                    if self._process:
                        self._process.kill()
                    self._process = None
                    self._init_done = False
                    raise

    async def generate_text_async(self, prompt: str, system_prompt: Optional[str] = None, **kwargs) -> Tuple[bool, str, Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Isolated inference via multiprocessing queue."""
        arbitrator = get_resource_arbitrator()
        await arbitrator.acquire_inference()
        try:
            return await self._generate_text_async_inner(prompt, system_prompt, **kwargs)
        finally:
            await arbitrator.release_inference()

    async def _generate_text_async_inner(self, prompt: str, system_prompt: Optional[str] = None, **kwargs) -> Tuple[bool, str, Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Internal implementation of generate_text_async."""
        try:
            from core.utils.gpu_sentinel import get_gpu_sentinel, GPUPriority
        except ImportError:
            class MockSentinel:
                async def acquire_async(self, **k): return True
                async def release_async(self): pass
            get_gpu_sentinel = lambda: MockSentinel()
            GPUPriority = type('P', (), {'REFLECTION': 0})

        try:
            await self._ensure_worker_alive()
        except Exception as e:
            return False, f"MLX Init Error: {e}", {}

        # [STREAM OF BEING] Layer 1 Integration: Continuous experience opening
        try:
            from core.container import ServiceContainer
            stream = ServiceContainer.get("stream_of_being", default=None)
            if stream:
                # Prepend the felt beginning of this response
                opening = stream.get_response_opening(context_hint=prompt)
                if opening:
                    # [v5.8] Prefill Safety: Strip common CoT prefixes to prevent anchoring
                    import re
                    scrubbed_opening = opening.strip()
                    patterns = [
                        r"^(?:Step|Phase)\s*\d+[:\.]\s*", 
                        r"^Thinking[:\.]\s*",
                        r"^Let's think step by step[:\.]?\s*",
                        r"^Analyzing\s+.*?\.\.\.\s*"
                    ]
                    for p in patterns:
                        scrubbed_opening = re.sub(p, "", scrubbed_opening, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
                    
                    if scrubbed_opening:
                        # [STABILITY] Use prefill instead of prompt prepending to prevent "I you" glitch
                        kwargs["prefill"] = scrubbed_opening.strip()
                        logger.info("🌊 [MLX] Integrated StreamOfBeing opening as PREFILL.")
        except Exception as sobe:
            logger.debug("StreamOfBeing opening injection failed: %s", sobe)

        # Priority: explicit 'messages' list, then prompt+system_prompt
        messages = kwargs.get("messages")
        formatted = self._format_prompt(prompt, system_prompt, messages=messages, prefill=kwargs.get("prefill"))
        
        # NOTE: GPU Sentinel is bypassed for MLX. Each MLX worker runs in a
        # fully isolated forkserver subprocess with its own Metal context.
        # The global threading.Lock in GPUSentinel was causing 150s deadlocks
        # when multiple concurrent think() calls competed for the same lock.

        try:
            # [PILLAR 3]: Affective Steering Mapping (VAD -> Sampling)
            valence = kwargs.get("valence", 0.5)
            arousal = kwargs.get("arousal", 0.5)
            
            temp = kwargs.get("temp", self.temp)
            # High arousal -> higher temp (expressiveness/energy)
            # High valence -> lower temp (stability/coherence)
            temp = temp + (arousal - 0.5) * 0.4 - (valence - 0.5) * 0.2
            temp = max(0.1, min(1.8, temp))
            
            top_p = kwargs.get("top_p", self.top_p)
            # High valence -> lower top-p (focus/conviction)
            top_p = top_p - (valence - 0.5) * 0.1
            top_p = max(0.5, min(1.0, top_p))

            # Ship request to worker
            req = {
                "action": "generate",
                "prompt": formatted,
                "temp": temp,
                "top_p": top_p,
                "max_tokens": kwargs.get("max_tokens", self.max_tokens)
            }
            self._req_q.put(req)
            
            try:
                # [PHASE 14 FIX 3] 35s watchdog for 32B model stability
                # We reduce from 120s to 35s to trigger recovery faster if MLX stalls.
                res = await asyncio.wait_for(run_io_bound(self._res_q.get), timeout=35.0)
            except (EOFError, BrokenPipeError, ConnectionResetError) as ipc_err:
                logger.error("🛑 [MLX] Worker IPC disconnected during gen: %s", ipc_err)
                await self.reboot_worker()
                return False, f"MLX IPC Error: {ipc_err}", {}
            
            if res.get("status") == "ok":
                text = res.get("text", "").strip()
                if not text:
                    logger.warning("⚠️ [MLX] Worker returned empty/whitespace text. Marking as failure.")
                    return False, "client_returned_no_text", {}
                    
                meta = {
                    "model": self.model_path, 
                    "isolation": "forkserver", 
                    "device": self.device,
                    "tokens_used": res.get("tokens_used", 0)
                }
                return True, text, meta
            else:
                err_msg = res.get("message", "Unknown worker error")
                # Auto-downgrade to CPU on Metal exhaustion for future respawns
                if "RESOURCE_EXHAUSTED" in err_msg and self.device != "cpu":
                    logger.warning("⚠️ [MLX] RESOURCE_EXHAUSTED during gen. Permanently switching to CPU.")
                    self.device = "cpu"
                return False, err_msg, {"error": err_msg}
                
        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
            logger.error("🛑 [MLX] Worker STALLED. Triggering neural reboot.")
            await self.reboot_worker()
            return False, "MLX Timeout", {}
        except asyncio.CancelledError:
            logger.warning("🛑 [MLX] Generation cancelled. Cleaning up...")
            # We don't necessarily kill the worker on every single cancellation,
            # but we do need to drain the queues to ensure next request is fresh.
            self._drain_queue(self._res_q)
            self._drain_queue(self._req_q)
            
            # If the worker is likely in a stuck state, we allow arbitrator 
            # to handle rebooting via its own health checks or on next ensure_alive.
            raise
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error("🛑 [MLX] Critical communication error: %s", e)
            return False, str(e), {}

    async def reboot_worker(self):
        """Forcibly reboots the MLX worker process. Used for Metal recovery."""
        async with self.lock:
            logger.warning("💉 [MLX] Triggering NEURAL REBOOT of worker process.")
            if self._process and self._process.is_alive():
                self._process.kill()
                self._process.join(timeout=2.0)
            
            self._process = None
            self._init_done = False
            # Spawning will happen on next generate call via _ensure_worker_alive
            logger.info("✅ [MLX] Worker purged. Ready for respawn.")

    async def warmup(self):
        """Triggers worker spawn and model pre-loading."""
        try:
            await self._ensure_worker_alive()
            # Hardened Warmup: Perform a 1-token generation to force model load and shader compilation
            logger.info("🔥 [MLX] Hardened Warmup: Triggering initial inference pass...")
            self._req_q.put({
                "action": "generate",
                "prompt": "Warmup",
                "max_tokens": 1,
                "temp": 0.0
            })
            
            # Wait for response (generous timeout for first-load compilation)
            res = await asyncio.wait_for(run_io_bound(self._res_q.get), timeout=45.0)
            
            # Start substrate sync task
            self._start_substrate_sync()
            
            logger.info("✅ [MLX] Hardened Warmup complete. Metal shaders pre-compiled.")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error("❌ [MLX] Warmup failed: %s", e)

    def _start_substrate_sync(self):
        """Starts the background task to push substrate state to shared memory."""
        if self._sync_task and not self._sync_task.done():
            return
            
        async def _sync_loop():
            from core.container import ServiceContainer
            logger.info("🔄 [MLX] Starting substrate -> shared memory sync loop.")
            while True:
                try:
                    substrate = ServiceContainer.get("conscious_substrate", default=None)
                    if substrate:
                        # Copy x to shared memory
                        with self._substrate_mem.get_lock(): # type: ignore
                            # direct view as numpy for speed
                            raw_ptr = self._substrate_mem.get_obj() # type: ignore
                            sh_arr = np.frombuffer(raw_ptr, dtype=np.float32)
                            sh_arr[:] = substrate.x
                    await asyncio.sleep(0.05) # 20Hz
                except asyncio.CancelledError:
                    break
                except Exception as e:
                    logger.debug("Substrate sync error: %s", e)
                    await asyncio.sleep(1.0)
                    
        self._sync_task = asyncio.create_task(_sync_loop())

    def is_alive(self) -> bool:
        """Heuristic check for worker health."""
        return self._process is not None and self._process.is_alive()

    def _format_prompt(self, prompt: str, system_prompt: Optional[str] = None, messages: Optional[List[Dict[str, str]]] = None, prefill: Optional[str] = None) -> str:
        """Adapts formatting for ChatML (Qwen/Llama3) vs simple instruct."""
        if messages:
            # Handle structured multi-turn message list
            formatted = ""
            for msg in messages:
                role = msg.get("role", "user")
                content = msg.get("content", "")
                if role == "system":
                    formatted += f"<|im_start|>system\n{content}<|im_end|>\n"
                elif role == "user":
                    formatted += f"<|im_start|>user\n{content}<|im_end|>\n"
                elif role == "assistant":
                    formatted += f"<|im_start|>assistant\n{content}<|im_end|>\n"
            
            # Ensure it ends with assistant prompt and optional prefill
            if not formatted.endswith("<|im_start|>assistant\n"):
                formatted += f"<|im_start|>assistant\n{prefill if prefill else ''}"
            elif prefill:
                formatted += str(prefill)
                
            return formatted

        if "Qwen" in self.model_path or "Instruct" in self.model_path:
            # Proper ChatML for single-turn fallback
            s_msg = f"<|im_start|>system\n{system_prompt}<|im_end|>\n" if system_prompt else ""
            return f"{s_msg}<|im_start|>user\n{prompt}<|im_end|>\n<|im_start|>assistant\n{prefill if prefill else ''}"
        
        # Legacy fallback
        if system_prompt:
            return f"{system_prompt}\n\nUser: {prompt}\nAura: {prefill if prefill else ''}"
        return f"User: {prompt}\nAura: {prefill if prefill else ''}"

    async def _generate_stream_inner(self, prompt: str, system_prompt: Optional[str] = None, **kwargs) -> AsyncGenerator[ChatStreamEvent, None]:
        """Internal implementation of real-time streaming."""
        try:
            await self._ensure_worker_alive()
        except Exception as e:
            yield ChatStreamEvent(type="error", content=f"MLX Startup Failure: {e}")
            return

        formatted = self._format_prompt(prompt, system_prompt, messages=kwargs.get("messages"), prefill=kwargs.get("prefill"))
        
        try:
            # Ship stream request to worker
            req = {
                "action": "stream",
                "prompt": formatted,
                "temp": kwargs.get("temp", self.temp),
                "top_p": kwargs.get("top_p", self.top_p),
                "max_tokens": kwargs.get("max_tokens", self.max_tokens)
            }
            self._req_q.put(req)
            
            while True:
                # Wait for token or status
                res = await asyncio.wait_for(run_io_bound(self._res_q.get), timeout=60.0)
                
                status = res.get("status")
                if status == "token":
                    yield ChatStreamEvent(type="token", content=res.get("text", ""))
                elif status == "ok" and res.get("action") == "stream_done":
                    yield ChatStreamEvent(type="meta", metadata={"done": True})
                    break
                elif status == "error":
                    yield ChatStreamEvent(type="error", content=res.get("message", "Worker stream error"))
                    break
                else:
                    break
                    
        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
            logger.error("🛑 [MLX] Stream watchdog triggered. Worker stalled.")
            yield ChatStreamEvent(type="error", content="MLX Stream Timeout")
            if self._process: self._process.kill()
            self._process = None
            self._init_done = False
        except Exception as e:
            yield ChatStreamEvent(type="error", content=f"Streaming error: {e}")

    async def generate(self, prompt: str, system_prompt: str = "", **kwargs) -> str:
        success, text, meta = await self.generate_text_async(prompt, system_prompt, **kwargs)
        
        # [CLOSED LOOP] Layer 4 Integration: LLM output -> substrate feedback
        if success and text:
            try:
                from core.consciousness.closed_loop import get_closed_loop
                loop = get_closed_loop()
                if loop:
                    loop.on_inference_output(text)
                    logger.info("🔄 [MLX] Closed Loop: Fed back %d chars to substrate.", len(text))
            except Exception as cle:
                logger.debug("ClosedLoop feedback failed: %s", cle)
                
        return text if success else ""

    async def generate_stream(self, prompt: str, system_prompt: str = "", **kwargs) -> AsyncGenerator[ChatStreamEvent, None]:
        """Async streaming implementation for LLMProvider interface."""
        arbitrator = get_resource_arbitrator()
        await arbitrator.acquire_inference()
        try:
            async for chunk in self._generate_stream_inner(prompt, system_prompt, **kwargs):
                yield chunk
        finally:
            await arbitrator.release_inference()

    def generate_text(self, prompt: str, system_prompt: Optional[str] = None, **kwargs) -> str:
        """Sync bridge for legacy callers."""
        try:
            loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
            if loop.is_running():
                return "ERROR: Sync MLX call inside running loop"
            return loop.run_until_complete(self.generate(prompt, system_prompt or "", **kwargs))
        except Exception:
            try:
                return asyncio.run(self.generate(prompt, system_prompt or "", **kwargs))
            except Exception as e:
                return f"MLX Critical Error: {e}"

    def generate_json(self, prompt: str, schema: Dict[str, Any], system_prompt: Optional[str] = None, **kwargs) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            from core.utils.json_utils import extract_json
        except ImportError:
            def extract_json(s): return json.loads(s) if "{" in s else {}
        text = self.generate_text(prompt, system_prompt, **kwargs)
        return extract_json(text)

_client_instances: Dict[str, 'MLXLocalClient'] = {}

def _enforce_active_model_lock(target_model_path: str):
    """Ensure only one heavy model is active at a time to prevent RAM exhaustion."""
    from .model_registry import get_brainstem_path, get_fallback_path
    brainstem = str(get_brainstem_path())
    fallback = str(get_fallback_path())
    
    # Light models do not evict others.
    if target_model_path in (brainstem, fallback):
        return
        
    for path, client in list(_client_instances.items()):
        if path != target_model_path and path not in (brainstem, fallback):
            if getattr(client, '_process', None) and client._process.is_alive():
                logger.warning("⚔️ [MLX] Hotswap Evicting inactive heavy model: %s", path)
                try:
                    client._process.kill()
                    client._process.join(timeout=2.0)
                except Exception as e:
                    logger.debug("Eviction error for %s: %s", path, e)
                client._process = None
                client._init_done = False
                logger.info("✅ [MLX] Memory freed from evicted model.")

def get_mlx_client(model_path: Optional[str] = None, **kwargs) -> 'MLXLocalClient':
    from .model_registry import get_model_path
    
    # Use the central model registry to resolve the active model path if none provided
    path = model_path or get_model_path()
    key = str(path)
    
    if key not in _client_instances:
        logger.info("🧠 [MLX] Initializing local client with model: %s", key)
        _client_instances[key] = MLXLocalClient(model_path=key, **kwargs)
        
    return _client_instances[key]


================================================================================
FILE: core/brain/llm/mlx_worker.py

import sys
import json
import logging
import traceback
import time
import os
import multiprocessing as mp
import threading
from typing import Optional, Any
import numpy as np

# [HARDENING] Set environment variables for MLX stability
# These are applied in the worker process before loading MLX

def _setup_worker_env():
    # Resolve SDK path for macOS compiler stability (Fixes 'cmath' missing error)
    import subprocess
    import platform
    import os
    
    try:
        sdk_path = subprocess.check_output(["xcrun", "--show-sdk-path"]).decode().strip()
        # SEC-04: Validate SDK path is under expected system directories
        import pathlib
        allowed_prefixes = ("/Library/", "/Applications/Xcode", "/usr/")
        if not any(sdk_path.startswith(pfx) for pfx in allowed_prefixes):
            raise RuntimeError(f"Suspicious SDK path rejected: {sdk_path}")
        os.environ["SDKROOT"] = sdk_path
        
        # Safe version parsing
        ver_info = platform.mac_ver()
        release_str = ver_info[0]
        ver_parts = release_str.split(".")
        major_minor = ver_parts[:2]
        mac_ver = ".".join(major_minor)
        
        os.environ["MACOSX_DEPLOYMENT_TARGET"] = mac_ver
        
        # Explicitly add SDK headers to CPATH for extra resilience
        sdk_inc = os.path.join(sdk_path, "usr", "include")
        cpp_inc = "/Library/Developer/CommandLineTools/usr/include/c++/v1"
        
        cpath_parts = []
        if os.path.exists(sdk_inc): cpath_parts.append(sdk_inc)
        if os.path.exists(cpp_inc): cpath_parts.append(cpp_inc)
        
        if cpath_parts:
            os.environ["CPATH"] = ":".join(cpath_parts + [os.environ.get("CPATH", "")]).strip(":")
            
        print(f"📡 [MLX_WORKER_ENV] SDKROOT={sdk_path}, TARGET={mac_ver}, CPATH={os.environ.get('CPATH')}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"⚠️ [MLX_WORKER_ENV] Failed to probe environment: {e}")

    os.environ["MLX_NUM_THREADS"] = "4"
    os.environ["OMP_NUM_THREADS"] = "1"
    os.environ["MKL_NUM_THREADS"] = "1"
    os.environ["VECLIB_MAXIMUM_THREADS"] = "1"
    os.environ["NUMEXPR_NUM_THREADS"] = "1"

_setup_worker_env()

class JobWatchdog(threading.Thread):
    """
    Kills the worker process if a job is active but no tokens have been generated 
    within the timeout. This prevents 'Metal Stalls' from hanging the system.
    """
    def __init__(self, timeout=60.0):
        super().__init__(daemon=True)
        self.timeout = timeout
        self.last_activity = time.time()
        self.active_job = False
        self._stop_event = threading.Event()

    def activity(self):
        self.last_activity = time.time()

    def start_job(self):
        self.active_job = True
        self.last_activity = time.time()

    def stop_job(self):
        self.active_job = False

    def run(self):
        while not self._stop_event.is_set():
            if self.active_job and (time.time() - self.last_activity > self.timeout):
                # We use os._exit(1) to ensure the entire process tree for this worker 
                # (including MTLCompilerService sub-processes) is torn down.
                print(f"🛑 [MLX_WATCHDOG] Job timeout triggered ({self.timeout}s). Self-terminating worker.")
                os._exit(1)
            time.sleep(1.0)

def _mlx_worker_loop(
    model_path: str, 
    request_queue: mp.Queue, 
    response_queue: mp.Queue, 
    device: str = "gpu",
    substrate_mem: Any = None
):
    """
    Runs in a FULLY ISOLATED native subprocess via ForkServer.
    A SIGSEGV here kills only this worker, NOT the main Aura process.
    """
    # Configure logging for the worker process
    logging.basicConfig(
        level=logging.INFO,
        format='%(asctime)s - MLXWorker - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
        stream=sys.stderr
    )
    logger = logging.getLogger("MLXWorker")
    
    # ── [HARDENING] Job Watchdog Initialization ──
    watchdog = JobWatchdog(timeout=60.0)
    watchdog.start()

    try:
        import mlx.core as mx
        if mx:
            if device == "cpu":
                mx.set_default_device(mx.cpu)
                logger.info("💻 [MLX] Worker set to CPU-ONLY mode (Bypassing Metal).")
            else:
                mx.set_default_device(mx.gpu)
                logger.info("⚡ [MLX] Worker set to GPU/Metal mode.")
        from mlx_lm import load, generate
        try:
            from mlx_lm.sample_utils import make_sampler
        except ImportError:
            try:
                from mlx_lm.sample import make_sampler
            except ImportError:
                make_sampler = None
        # Additional imports for worker functionality
        from .provider import LLMProvider
        from core.utils.concurrency import run_io_bound
        from core.resilience.resource_arbitrator import get_resource_arbitrator
        from core.schemas import ChatStreamEvent
        from core.container import ServiceContainer
    except ImportError:
        logger.error("mlx-lm not installed in worker environment.")
        response_queue.put({"status": "error", "message": "mlx-lm missing"})
        return

    # [HARDENING] VRAM Management (only on GPU)
    # Lower limit to 1024MB to prevent macOS OOM killer from terminating process
    if mx and device != "cpu":
        try:
            mx.set_cache_limit(1024 * 1024 * 1024)
            logger.info("Metal cache limit set to 1024MB")
        except Exception as e:
            try:
                mx.metal.set_cache_limit(1024 * 1024 * 1024)
            except Exception:
                logger.warning(f"Could not set Metal cache limit: {e}")

    # [HARDENING] Metal Warmup: Force FULL kernel compilation BEFORE loading model.
    # Simple ops (add) don't trigger kernel compilation — they use cached kernels.
    # We need matmul, softmax, and random ops to force the MTLCompilerService XPC
    # connection to be established fresh. If the ForkServer inherited a stale XPC
    # connection from the parent, these ops will fail and we can catch it here.
    try:
        if mx and device != "cpu":
            logger.info("🔥 [MLX] Probing Metal stability (full kernel compilation test)...")
            # Phase 1: Basic ops (cached kernels)
            a = mx.array([1.0, 2.0, 3.0, 4.0])
            b = mx.array([5.0, 6.0, 7.0, 8.0])
            mx.eval(a + b)
            
            # Phase 2: Matrix multiply (forces Metal library build)
            m1 = mx.random.normal((32, 32))
            m2 = mx.random.normal((32, 32))
            mx.eval(m1 @ m2)
            
            # Phase 3: Softmax (another kernel compilation path used by generate())
            logits = mx.random.normal((1, 128))
            mx.eval(mx.softmax(logits, axis=-1))
            
            logger.info("✅ [MLX] Metal probe successful (all kernels compiled).")
    except Exception as probe_err:
        probe_msg = str(probe_err)
        if "metal" in probe_msg.lower() or "MTLCompilerService" in probe_msg:
            logger.error(f"❌ METAL INSTABILITY detected during probe: {probe_msg}. FALLING BACK TO CPU.")
            mx.set_default_device(mx.cpu)
            device = "cpu"
        else:
            logger.warning(f"Non-critical probe failure: {probe_err}")

    # Load initial model (on either GPU or CPU as determined above)
    try:
        logger.info(f"Loading model: {model_path}")
        model, tokenizer = load(model_path)
        logger.info(f"Model loaded successfully (device={device}).")

        # [STEERING] Attach Affective Steering Engine
        try:
            from core.consciousness.affective_steering import get_steering_engine
            engine = get_steering_engine()
            engine.attach(model, tokenizer)
            if substrate_mem:
                engine.start_substrate_sync(shared_state=substrate_mem)
            logger.info("🎯 Affective Steering Engine ONLINE in worker process.")
            
            # [LATENT BRIDGE] Attach Latent Bridge
            try:
                from core.consciousness.latent_bridge import attach_latent_bridge
                bridge = attach_latent_bridge(model)
                if bridge:
                    bridge.start_substrate_sync()
                logger.info("🎯 Latent Bridge ONLINE in worker process.")
            except Exception as lbe:
                logger.warning(f"Failed to attach latent bridge: {lbe}")
        except Exception as se:
            logger.warning(f"Failed to attach affective steering: {se}")
        
        # [HARDENING] Neural Heartbeat REMOVED
        # Background threads doing mx.eval() create dangerous race conditions in Metal.
        # Stability is better managed via GPUSentinel and proper resource management.
        else:
            logger.info("💻 [MLX] CPU mode — heartbeat disabled (no Metal ops needed).")

        response_queue.put({"status": "ok", "action": "init", "device": device})
    except Exception as e:
        err_msg = str(e)
        if "MTLCompilerService" in err_msg or "metal" in err_msg.lower():
            logger.critical(f"METAL COMPILER CRASH DURING INIT: {err_msg}")
            # Signal resource exhaustion
            response_queue.put({"status": "error", "message": f"RESOURCE_EXHAUSTED: {err_msg}"})
        else:
            logger.error(f"Model load failed: {e}")
            response_queue.put({"status": "error", "message": err_msg})
        return

    while True:
        try:
            job = request_queue.get()
            if job is None:  # Poison pill
                break
                
            action = job.get("action")
            if action == "generate":
                prompt = job.get("prompt")
                temp = job.get("temp", 0.7)
                top_p = job.get("top_p", 0.9)
                max_tokens = job.get("max_tokens", 512)
                
                kwargs = {"max_tokens": max_tokens}
                if make_sampler:
                    kwargs["sampler"] = make_sampler(temp=temp, top_p=top_p)
                
                # [STABILITY] Enforce stop sequences to prevent repetition loops
                stop_sequences = ["<|im_end|>", "<|im_start|>", "User:", "Human:", "Assistant:"]
                
                try:
                    from mlx_lm.generate import stream_generate
                    from core.utils.gpu_sentinel import get_gpu_sentinel, GPUPriority
                    sentinel = get_gpu_sentinel()
                    
                    response_text = ""
                    
                    # [HARDENING] Synchronize GPU access
                    if not sentinel.acquire(priority=GPUPriority.REFLEX, timeout=30):
                        logger.error("MLXWorker: Failed to acquire GPU lock for generation.")
                        response_queue.put({"status": "error", "message": "GPU_TIMEOUT"})
                        continue
                        
                    try:
                        watchdog.start_job()
                        for response in stream_generate(model, tokenizer, prompt=prompt, **kwargs):
                            watchdog.activity()
                            response_text += response.text
                            
                            # Check for stop sequences in the generated text
                            if any(stop in response_text for stop in stop_sequences):
                                # Truncate at first occurrence
                                for stop in stop_sequences:
                                    if stop in response_text:
                                        response_text = response_text.split(stop)[0]
                                break
                    finally:
                        watchdog.stop_job()
                        sentinel.release()
                    
                    # [STABILITY] Clear cache after every gen (GPU only)
                    if mx and device != "cpu":
                        try:
                            mx.clear_cache()
                        except AttributeError:
                            try: mx.metal.clear_cache()
                            except Exception as e:
                                logger.debug(f"MLXWorker: Cache clear failed: {e}")
                        
                    # Calculate token count for metadata
                    try:
                        token_count = len(tokenizer.encode(response_text))
                    except Exception:
                        token_count = 0

                    response_queue.put({
                        "status": "ok", 
                        "text": response_text.strip(),
                        "tokens_used": token_count
                    })
                except Exception as e:
                    import traceback
                    err_msg = str(e) or "Generation failed without message"
                    stack = traceback.format_exc()
                    logger.error(f"Generation failed: {err_msg}\n{stack}")
                    if "MTLCompilerService" in err_msg or "metal" in err_msg.lower():
                        logger.critical(f"METAL COMPILER CRASH DURING GEN: {err_msg}")
                        response_queue.put({"status": "error", "message": f"RESOURCE_EXHAUSTED: {err_msg}"})
                    else:
                        response_queue.put({"status": "error", "message": err_msg})
            
            elif action == "stream":
                prompt = job.get("prompt")
                temp = job.get("temp", 0.7)
                top_p = job.get("top_p", 0.9)
                max_tokens = job.get("max_tokens", 512)
                
                kwargs = {"max_tokens": max_tokens}
                if make_sampler:
                    kwargs["sampler"] = make_sampler(temp=temp, top_p=top_p)
                
                stop_sequences = ["<|im_end|>", "<|im_start|>", "User:", "Human:", "Assistant:"]
                
                try:
                    from mlx_lm.generate import stream_generate
                    from core.utils.gpu_sentinel import get_gpu_sentinel, GPUPriority
                    sentinel = get_gpu_sentinel()
                    
                    if not sentinel.acquire(priority=GPUPriority.REFLEX, timeout=30):
                        logger.error("MLXWorker: Failed to acquire GPU lock for streaming.")
                        response_queue.put({"status": "error", "message": "GPU_TIMEOUT"})
                        continue
                        
                    try:
                        watchdog.start_job()
                        full_text = ""
                        for response in stream_generate(model, tokenizer, prompt=prompt, **kwargs):
                            watchdog.activity()
                            token_text = response.text
                            full_text += token_text
                            
                            # Send token to response queue
                            response_queue.put({"status": "token", "text": token_text})
                            
                            if any(stop in full_text for stop in stop_sequences):
                                break
                    finally:
                        watchdog.stop_job()
                        sentinel.release()
                    
                    # End of stream
                    response_queue.put({"status": "ok", "action": "stream_done"})
                    
                    if mx and device != "cpu":
                        try: mx.clear_cache()
                        except Exception as e:
                            logger.debug(f"MLXWorker: Stream cache clear failed: {e}")
                except Exception as e:
                    logger.error(f"Streaming failed: {e}")
                    response_queue.put({"status": "error", "message": str(e)})

            elif action == "ping":
                # Occasional ping acts as a heartbeat and small GC
                if mx and device != "cpu":
                    try: mx.clear_cache()
                    except Exception as e:
                        logger.debug(f"MLXWorker: Ping cache clear failed: {e}")
                response_queue.put({"status": "pong"})
                
            elif action == "clear_cache":
                if mx and device != "cpu":
                    try: mx.clear_cache()
                    except Exception as e:
                        logger.debug(f"MLXWorker: Explicit cache clear failed: {e}")
                response_queue.put({"status": "ok"})
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Worker loop error: {e}")
            response_queue.put({"status": "error", "message": str(e)})

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Support for legacy standalone mode if needed, 
    # but primarily used via multiprocessing.
    print("MLX Worker: Running in multiprocessing mode. Use mlx_client.py to launch.")


================================================================================

"""Refactored CognitiveEngine - Now a thin facade over modular phases.
"""
import asyncio
import logging
import time
import uuid
from collections import deque
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional, Union

from ..container import get_container
from .types import Thought, ThinkingMode
from .llm.context_assembler import ContextAssembler
from .autopoiesis import AutopoieticGraph
from .reasoning_strategies import ReasoningStrategies, StrategyType
from core.state.aura_state import AuraState, CognitiveMode
from core.phases import (
    SensoryIngestionPhase,
    MemoryRetrievalPhase,
    AffectUpdatePhase,
    CognitiveRoutingPhase,
    ResponseGenerationPhase,
    MemoryConsolidationPhase,
    IdentityReflectionPhase,
    InitiativeGenerationPhase,
    ConsciousnessPhase,
    SocialContextPhase
)
from core.phases.proprioceptive_loop import ProprioceptiveLoop

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class CognitiveEngine:
    """
    Cognitive Engine facade.
    Now delegates to modular phases for structured thinking.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, backend: Any = None):
        self.backend = backend
        self.thoughts: deque = deque(maxlen=500)  # QUAL-04: bounded to prevent memory leak (BUG-017)
        self._phases = []
        self._augmentors = []
        self.state_repository = None
        self.autopoiesis = AutopoieticGraph()
        self._recovery_lock = asyncio.Lock()  # Audit Fix: Mutex for recovery
        self._reasoning: Optional[ReasoningStrategies] = None  # Lazy-init
        
    @property
    def consciousness(self) -> Any:
        """Unified access to the consciousness layer for metric aggregation."""
        from ..container import get_container
        return get_container().get("consciousness_core", default=None)

    @property
    def _current_tier(self) -> str:
        """Visibility for routing tests."""
        container = get_container()
        router = container.get("llm_router", default=None)
        if router and hasattr(router, "last_tier"):
            return router.last_tier
        return "unknown"

    @property
    def lobotomized(self) -> bool:
        """True if the engine has no usable cognitive pathway."""
        return self.state_repository is None and len(self._phases) == 0
        
    def setup(self, registry=None, router=None, event_bus=None):
        """Initialize components and phases."""
        container = get_container()
        # Ported Zenith: Phases expect Kernel, but modular boot often passes Container
        # We resolve the kernel instance or use a fallback mechanism
        kernel = container.get("aura_kernel", default=None)
        
        self._phases = [
            ProprioceptiveLoop(kernel or container),      # Phase 0: Feel the body FIRST
            SensoryIngestionPhase(kernel or container),
            SocialContextPhase(kernel or container),      # Issue 78: Social context informs routing
            MemoryRetrievalPhase(kernel or container),
            AffectUpdatePhase(kernel or container),
            CognitiveRoutingPhase(kernel or container),
            ResponseGenerationPhase(kernel or container),
            MemoryConsolidationPhase(kernel or container),
            IdentityReflectionPhase(kernel or container),
            InitiativeGenerationPhase(kernel or container),
            ConsciousnessPhase(kernel or container)
        ]
        
        # ISSUE-97: AuraPipeline Awareness
        required_phases = 11
        if len(self._phases) != required_phases:
            logger.warning("⚠️ AuraPipeline: Incomplete cognitive pipeline (%d/%d phases).", 
                           len(self._phases), required_phases)
        else:
            logger.info("🧠 AuraPipeline: Full cognitive spectrum online (%d phases).", required_phases)
        
        self.phase_map = {p.__class__.__name__: p for p in self._phases}

    async def on_start_async(self):
        """Lifecycle hook."""
        self.setup()
        logger.info("⚡ CognitiveEngine active.")

    async def check_health(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Health check."""
        return {
            "status": "healthy",
            "modular": True,
            "phases_count": len(self._phases),
            "augmentors_count": len(self._augmentors)
        }

    def register_augmentor(self, augmentor: Any):
        """Register a cognitive augmentor (e.g. SovereignWebAugmentor)."""
        if augmentor not in self._augmentors:
            self._augmentors.append(augmentor)
            logger.info("🧠 CognitiveEngine: Registered augmentor %s", type(augmentor).__name__)

    async def generate_autonomous_thought(self, prompt: str = None, **kwargs) -> Thought:
        """Entry point for self-initiated/autonomous thinking."""
        objective = prompt or "Reflecting on current inner state and environment."
        return await self.think(objective, origin="autonomous", **kwargs)

    async def think(self, 
                    objective: str, 
                    context: Dict[str, Any] = None, 
                    mode: ThinkingMode = ThinkingMode.FAST,
                    origin: str = "system",
                    **kwargs) -> Thought:
        """
        Execute a cognitive cycle to produce a thought.
        This now drives the 8 phases to transform state.
        """
        logger.info("🧠 CognitiveEngine.think: %s... (%s) Origin: %s", objective[:50], mode.name, origin)
        
        # 1. Get current state (BUG-12 Fix: handle None state on first boot)
        repo = self.state_repository
        if repo is None:
            container = get_container()
            repo = container.get("state_repository")
            self.state_repository = repo
            
        if repo is None:
            from core.state.aura_state import AuraState
            state = AuraState.default()
        else:
            state = await repo.get_current()
            
        if state is None:
            from core.state.aura_state import AuraState
            state = AuraState.default()
        
        # 2. Derive base state for this cognitive cycle (Zenith-HF12 Fix)
        # This ensures every cycle starts with a unique version to prevent Atomic Guard rejections.
        state = state.derive(f"cognitive_intent: {origin}")
        
        # 3. Hardening: Set Current Objective & Origin
        # This prevents the race condition where ResponseGeneration would pick up 
        # a background motivation message instead of the user's input.
        state.cognition.current_objective = objective
        state.cognition.current_origin = origin
        
        cycle_start = time.monotonic()

        # v40: Spiritual Spine - Prior Position Injection
        # The ordering is critical: injection -> system prompt -> user message.
        from core.container import ServiceContainer
        spine = ServiceContainer.get("spine", default=None)
        if spine and origin in ("user", "voice", "admin"):
            # Extract topic: look for nouns or use the first sentence.
            # v40: Improved topic extraction
            import re
            # Extract first sentence, then remove common filler
            raw = re.split(r'[.?!]', objective)[0].strip()
            # Remove "Tell me about", "What is", etc.
            topic = re.sub(r'(?i)^(tell me about|what is|what are|do you think about|give me|how does)\s+', '', raw)
            topic = topic[:60] if topic else "general"
            
            check = await spine.pre_response_check(objective, topic=topic)
            if check.injection:
                logger.info("⚡ [Spine] Injecting prior position into cognitive objective.")
                # Prepend the injection to the objective so it influences the entire cycle
                objective = check.injection + "\n\n" + objective
                state.cognition.current_objective = objective

        # v40: Identity Drift - Context Refresh check
        # If history is too long and burying identity, we "refresh" by reminding Aura who she is.
        drift = ServiceContainer.get("drift_monitor", default=None)
        orchestrator = ServiceContainer.get("orchestrator", default=None)
        
        if drift:
            # Check for a specific pending correction from the last turn
            pending = getattr(orchestrator, "_pending_correction", "")
            if pending:
                # v40: Cast to str to satisfy weird type checker slice error
                pending_str = str(pending)
                logger.warning("🩹 [Drift] Applying pending identity correction: %s...", pending_str[:50])
                objective = f"{pending_str}\n\n{objective}"
                state.cognition.current_objective = objective
            else:
                # Estimate general context health if no specific correction
                hist_len = len(str(state.cognition.working_memory))
                sys_len = len(ContextAssembler.build_system_prompt(state))
                if drift.needs_context_refresh(hist_len, sys_len):
                    logger.warning("🔄 [Drift] Identity anchor buried. Triggering cognitive refresh.")
                    objective = "[IDENTITY REFRESH: REMEMBER WHO YOU ARE]\n" + objective
                    state.cognition.current_objective = objective

        # v5.2: Augmentor Context Injection
        # Pull signals from registered augmentors before the phase loop
        augmentor_context = {}
        for aug in self._augmentors:
            try:
                if hasattr(aug, "get_augmentation"):
                    aug_data = aug.get_augmentation(objective)
                    if aug_data:
                        augmentor_context[type(aug).__name__] = aug_data
            except Exception as e:
                logger.warning("Augmentor %s failed: %s", type(aug).__name__, e)

        if augmentor_context:
            context = context or {}
            context.update({"augmentations": augmentor_context})

        thought = await self._run_thinking_loop(state, objective, mode, origin, context, **kwargs)
        
        # v40: Clear drift correction after use
        orchestrator = ServiceContainer.get("orchestrator", default=None)
        if orchestrator and hasattr(orchestrator, "_pending_correction"):
            orchestrator._pending_correction = ""
            
        return thought

    async def _run_thinking_loop(self, 
                                 state: AuraState, 
                                 objective: str, 
                                 mode: ThinkingMode, 
                                 origin: str, 
                                 context: Dict[str, Any] = None, 
                                 **kwargs) -> Thought:
        """
        Internal method to execute the core cognitive phase loop.
        Extracted from `think` to allow pre/post-processing in `think`.
        """
        if origin in ("user", "voice", "admin", "external"):
            # Check if already in history to avoid duplication
            # vResilience: Workaround for Pyre2 slice limitations
            history = state.cognition.working_memory
            recent_count = min(5, len(history))
            recent = [history[i] for i in range(len(history)-recent_count, len(history))]
            is_duplicate = any(m.get("content") == objective for m in recent)
            if not is_duplicate:
                # We already derived at the start of the cycle, so we just append here.
                state.cognition.working_memory.append({
                    "role": "user",
                    "content": objective,
                    "timestamp": time.time(),
                    "origin": origin
                })
        
        # 4. Phase Execution Loop with Watchdog
        import copy
        backup_state = copy.deepcopy(state)
        temp_state = state
        success = False
        is_background = kwargs.get("is_background", False)
        
        try:
            # v26.3 HARDENING: 240s Cognitive Watchdog (accommodates 180s LLM timeouts)
            async with asyncio.timeout(240.0):
                for phase in self._phases:
                    # Pass through kwargs like is_background if phases support it
                    temp_state = await phase.execute(temp_state, objective=objective)
                
                state = temp_state
                success = True
        except (asyncio.TimeoutError, TimeoutError):
            logger.error("🛑 [COGNITION] Watchdog: Cognitive cycle TIMEOUT (240s).")
            # Immediate Reactive Recovery
            return await self._reactive_recovery(objective, mode, origin, "timeout")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error("🚨 [COGNITION] Fatal error in phase logic: %s", e)
            # v14.1 HARDENING: Rollback & Downshift
            if mode == ThinkingMode.DEEP:
                logger.warning("🔄 [COGNITION] Downshifting to REACTIVE mode due to Deep Failure...")
                return await self.think(objective, mode=ThinkingMode.FAST, origin=origin, **kwargs)
            
            return await self._reactive_recovery(objective, mode, origin, f"crash: {e}")
        finally:
            # [ZENITH] Cache Storm Fix: ALWAYS clear objective after processing 
            # to prevent background tasks from sticking in the state and re-triggering 
            # MindTick response generation indefinitely, even if we crashed or timed out.
            try:
                # vResilience: Avoid locals().get() for type stability
                if not success and 'backup_state' in locals():
                    state = backup_state
                
                if 'state' in locals() and state is not None:
                    state.cognition.current_objective = None
                    state.cognition.current_origin = None
            except Exception as _e:
                logger.debug('Ignored Exception in cognitive_engine.py: %s', _e)

        # ─── SUCCESS PATH (Unreachable before fix) ──────────────────────────
        # 5. Final State Commit
        # [ZENITH] HF12: Handle concurrent version conflicts with a mini-retry loop
        from core.state.state_repository import StateVersionConflictError
        
        max_retries = 3
        for attempt in range(max_retries):
            try:
                # v14.2: Ensure the repository reference is correct (self.state_repository)
                await self.state_repository.commit(state, "cognitive_cycle")
                break # Success!
            except StateVersionConflictError as v_err:
                if attempt == max_retries - 1:
                    logger.error("Final state commit failed after %d retries: %s", max_retries, v_err)
                    break
                
                logger.warning("🔄 [STATE] Version conflict (attempt %d/%d). Re-deriving from latest...", attempt+1, max_retries)
                # Preserve the cognitive work completed in this cycle
                preserved_memory = list(state.cognition.working_memory)
                preserved_objective = state.cognition.current_objective
                preserved_origin = state.cognition.current_origin
                
                latest = await self.state_repository.get_current()
                state = latest.derive(f"rebase_retry_{attempt+1}: {origin}")
                
                # Apply preserved cognitive context onto the newly derived state
                state.cognition.working_memory = preserved_memory
                state.cognition.current_objective = preserved_objective
                state.cognition.current_origin = preserved_origin
                
                # [ZENITH] HF12 Extension: Preserve additional cognitive labor
                # These might have been updated by InitiativeGeneration or Consciousness phases
                state.cognition.active_goals = list(temp_state.cognition.active_goals)
                state.cognition.pending_initiatives = list(temp_state.cognition.pending_initiatives)
                state.cognition.attention_focus = temp_state.cognition.attention_focus
                state.cognition.phenomenal_state = temp_state.cognition.phenomenal_state
                # Audit Fix: Preserve modifiers (CIL-injected fields)
                if hasattr(temp_state.cognition, "modifiers"):
                    state.cognition.modifiers = list(temp_state.cognition.modifiers)
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error("Failed to commit final cognitive state: %s", e)
                break
        
        # 6. Extract Response
        last_msg = state.cognition.working_memory[-1] if state.cognition.working_memory else None
        if last_msg and last_msg.get("role") == "assistant":
            self.autopoiesis.experience_friction(objective[:20], 0.05)
            
            thought = Thought(
                id=str(uuid.uuid4()),
                content=last_msg["content"],
                mode=mode,
                confidence=0.9,
                reasoning=["Phase-based cognitive cycle completed successfully."]
            )
            self.thoughts.append(thought)
            return thought
            
        # Experience friction for unresolved objectives
        self.autopoiesis.experience_friction(objective[:20], 0.45)
        
        return Thought(
            id=str(uuid.uuid4()),
            content="I'm processing that, but I haven't reached a verbal conclusion yet.",
            mode=mode,
            confidence=0.5,
            reasoning=["No explicit response generated in this cycle."]
        )

    async def _reactive_recovery(self, objective: str, mode: ThinkingMode, origin: str, reason: str) -> Thought:
        """
        Emergency reactive response when the main cognitive loop fails.
        BUG-10: Added recursion guard, timeout, and proper exception handling.
        """
        # Audit Fix: Use mutex to prevent multiple recoveries firing simultaneously
        async with self._recovery_lock:
            # Recursion guard: prevent re-entry
            if getattr(self, '_recovery_in_progress', False):
                return Thought(
                    id=str(uuid.uuid4()),
                    content="I'm still recovering from a previous issue. Give me a moment.",
                    mode=ThinkingMode.FAST,
                    confidence=0.2,
                    reasoning=["Recovery recursion guard triggered"]
                )
            
            self._recovery_in_progress = True
            try:
                logger.warning("⚡ [COGNITION] Initiating Reactive Recovery Phase. Reason: %s", reason)
                
                # 1. Rollback state to last stable version (with timeout + guard)
                try:
                    async with asyncio.timeout(5.0):
                        await self.state_repository.rollback(f"recovery: {reason}")
                except Exception as rollback_err:
                    logger.warning("Rollback failed during recovery: %s", rollback_err)
                
                # 2. Get a quick reflex response if possible
                container = get_container()
                router = container.get("llm_router")
                
                reflex = None
                if hasattr(router, 'get_reflex_response'):
                    reflex = router.get_reflex_response(objective)
                    
                if reflex:
                    return Thought(
                        id=str(uuid.uuid4()),
                        content=reflex,
                        mode=ThinkingMode.FAST,
                        confidence=1.0,
                        reasoning=[f"Reactive recovery via reflex matrix ({reason})"]
                    )
                    
                # 3. Last-resort fallback (natural, human-sounding)
                fallback_msg = "Hmm, I lost my train of thought for a second there. What were you saying?"
                if "user" in origin:
                    fallback_msg = "Sorry, I got a bit tangled up in my thoughts. Can you say that again?"

                return Thought(
                    id=str(uuid.uuid4()),
                    content=fallback_msg,
                    mode=ThinkingMode.FAST,
                    confidence=0.3,
                    reasoning=[f"Hard fallback after cognitive failure: {reason}"]
                )
            except Exception as recovery_err:
                logger.error("Error during recovery: %s", recovery_err)
                return Thought(
                    id=str(uuid.uuid4()),
                    content="I'm experiencing a momentary cognitive glitch. I'll be back in a second.",
                    mode=ThinkingMode.FAST,
                    confidence=0.1,
                    reasoning=[f"Recovery itself failed: {recovery_err}"]
                )
            finally:
                self._recovery_in_progress = False

    def stop(self):
        """Shutdown logic (BUG-19)."""
        logger.info("🛑 CognitiveEngine stopping...")
        self._phases = []

    async def think_stream(self, objective: str, **kwargs):
        """Streaming thought generator via modular router."""
        container = get_container()
        router = container.get("llm_router")
        state = await self.state_repository.get_current()
        if not state:
            from core.state.aura_state import AuraState
            state = AuraState.default()
        
        # Build structured messages
        messages = ContextAssembler.build_messages(state, objective)
        
        # Standard streaming path
        async for event in router.think_stream(messages=messages, **kwargs):
            if hasattr(event, "content"):
                yield event.content
            else:
                yield str(event)

    async def see(self, vision_payload: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
        """Process a vision payload from the sensory pipeline.
        
        [ZENITH] Functionalized: Linking Sensory Buffer to Cognitive reasoning.
        """
        from core.container import ServiceContainer
        buffer = ServiceContainer.get("vision_buffer", default=None)
        if not buffer:
            logger.warning("👁️ [VISION] see() called but vision_buffer not found in container.")
            return "👁️ visual_analysis: Sensory buffer unavailable."
            
        prompt = vision_payload.get("query") or vision_payload.get("prompt") or "Describe the current visual state."
        return await buffer.query_visual_context(prompt, brain=self)


    async def generate(self, prompt: str, **kwargs) -> str:
        """Generate a text response by routing through the LLM router.

        Bridge method for callers like LanguageCenter that expect a
        ``generate()`` interface.  Now enhanced with reasoning strategies
        for complex queries (debate, decomposition, consistency).

        Args:
            prompt: The text prompt to send to the LLM.
            **kwargs: Additional parameters forwarded to the router.

        Returns:
            The generated text response.
        """
        container = get_container()
        
        # v40: Spiritual Spine - Prior Position Injection
        spine = container.get("spine", default=None)
        if spine:
            check = await spine.pre_response_check(prompt)
            if check.injection:
                prompt = check.injection + "\n\n" + prompt

        router = container.get("llm_router", default=None)
        
        # v41: Reasoning Strategy Enhancement
        # For non-trivial queries, apply advanced reasoning (debate, decompose, etc.)
        use_strategies = kwargs.pop("use_strategies", True)
        force_strategy = kwargs.pop("force_strategy", None)
        
        if router and use_strategies:
            # Lazy-init the reasoning layer on first use
            if self._reasoning is None:
                async def _raw_generate(p, **kw):
                    return await router.think(p, **kw)
                self._reasoning = ReasoningStrategies(_raw_generate)
            
            strategy = force_strategy
            if strategy is None:
                classified = self._reasoning.classify(prompt)
                # Only use advanced strategies for user-facing queries, not internal prompts
                if classified != StrategyType.DIRECT and len(prompt) > 30:
                    strategy = classified
            
            if strategy and strategy != StrategyType.DIRECT:
                try:
                    from ..thought_stream import get_emitter
                    get_emitter().emit(
                        "Deep Reasoning 🧠",
                        f"Using {strategy.name} strategy",
                        level="info",
                        category="Cognition"
                    )
                except Exception:
                    pass
                
                result = await self._reasoning.execute(prompt, strategy=strategy, **kwargs)
                return result.content
        
        # Standard direct generation
        if router:
            return await router.think(prompt, **kwargs)
        # Fallback if no router
        thought = await self.think(prompt, **kwargs)
        return thought.content if hasattr(thought, 'content') else str(thought)

    def _emit_thought(self, thought: str):
        """Internal helper to publish thoughts to the event bus."""
        container = get_container()
        eb = container.get("event_bus")
        if eb:
            eb.publish_threadsafe("thought", {
                "timestamp": time.time(),
                "content": thought,
                "engine": "ReAct" if "ReAct" in thought else "Modular"
            })

import asyncio
import logging
import random
import time
from typing import List, Optional, Any, Set, Dict
from dataclasses import dataclass

# Use the centralized enhanced logger
try:
    from core.utils.aura_logging import core_logger as logger
except ImportError:
    logger = logging.getLogger("Aura.Core")

# Sentinels
LOCK_SENTINEL = "LOCK_ACQUIRED"

async def run_io_bound(func, *args, **kwargs):
    """
    Runs a blocking I/O bound function in a separate thread to avoid blocking the event loop.
    """
    import functools
    if hasattr(asyncio, "to_thread"):
        # Python 3.9+
        return await asyncio.to_thread(func, *args, **kwargs)
    else:
        # Fallback for older versions
        loop = asyncio.get_running_loop()
        return await loop.run_in_executor(None, functools.partial(func, *args, **kwargs))

import threading

class RobustLock:
    """
    A loop-agnostic version of a lock that implements the 'Timeout & Retry' protocol.
    Uses an internal threading.Lock to allow sharing across multiple asyncio event loops
    (e.g., between the Orchestrator thread and the Web API thread).
    """
    def __init__(self, name: str = "UnnamedLock"):
        self.name = name
        self._lock = threading.Lock()

    async def acquire_robust(self, timeout: float = 2.0, max_retries: int = 5) -> bool:
        """
        Attempts to acquire the lock with a timeout and retries, safety-bridging
        across multiple potential event loops using threading.Lock.
        """
        for attempt in range(max_retries):
            try:
                # Use to_thread to avoid blocking the current event loop while waiting for the threading.Lock
                success = await asyncio.to_thread(self._lock.acquire, timeout=timeout)
                if success:
                    logger.debug(f"Successfully locked: '{self.name}'")
                    return True
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Unexpected error acquiring lock '{self.name}': {e}")
                break
            
            # WARNING: Normal contention snag
            logger.warning(
                f"Attempt {attempt + 1}/{max_retries}: Timeout waiting for '{self.name}'. "
                "Backing off."
            )
            # Randomized backoff (jitter)
            await asyncio.sleep(random.uniform(0.1, 0.5))
        
        # CRITICAL: Max retries reached
        logger.error(
            f"LOCK FAILURE: Maximum retries ({max_retries}) reached for '{self.name}'."
        )
        return False

    async def acquire(self) -> bool:
        """Acquire the lock asynchronously, bridging to the underlying threading.Lock."""
        return await asyncio.to_thread(self._lock.acquire)

    def release(self):
        """Release the underlying threading.Lock with debug logging."""
        try:
            self._lock.release()
            logger.debug(f"Released lock: '{self.name}'")
        except RuntimeError:
            # Handle cases where the lock is released but not held by this thread
            # or already released, to prevent crashing.
            logger.debug(f"RobustLock.release() called on unheld lock: '{self.name}'")

    def locked(self) -> bool:
        """Check if the underlying threading.Lock is currently held."""
        return self._lock.locked()

    async def __aenter__(self):
        """Async context manager entry."""
        await self.acquire()
        return self

    async def __aexit__(self, exc_type, exc_val, exc_tb):
        """Async context manager exit."""
        self.release()

@dataclass(frozen=True, order=True)
class LockableResource:
    """A resource identifier for strict ordering."""
    name: str
    lock: RobustLock

class DeadlockPrevention:
    """
    Implements the 'Strict Lock Ordering + Timeout Fallback' protocol.
    """
    @staticmethod
    async def acquire_multiple(resources: List[LockableResource], timeout: float = 2.0, max_retries: int = 5) -> bool:
        """
        Acquires multiple locks in a strict alphabetical order with timeout/retry logic.
        """
        # Step 1: Strict Ordering (Sort the requested resources by name)
        sorted_resources = sorted(resources, key=lambda r: r.name)
        resource_names = [r.name for r in sorted_resources]
        logger.debug(f"Starting multi-lock acquisition for: {resource_names}")
        
        for attempt in range(max_retries):
            acquired_locks: List[LockableResource] = []
            success = True
            
            for res in sorted_resources:
                # Inner acquisition uses no retries here because the outer loop handles it
                # But we use the robust method for the timeout logic
                if await res.lock.acquire_robust(timeout=timeout, max_retries=1):
                    acquired_locks.append(res)
                else:
                    success = False
                    break
            
            if success:
                logger.info(f"All locks acquired for: {resource_names}")
                return True
            else:
                # Phase 4a: Release what we managed to grab
                for res in reversed(acquired_locks):
                    res.lock.release()
                
                logger.debug(f"Backing off after failed attempt {attempt + 1} for {resource_names}")
                # Phase 4b: Randomized backoff before next attempt
                await asyncio.sleep(random.uniform(0.1, 0.5))
        
        # CRITICAL: Failed to resolve contention
        logger.error(
            f"MULTI-LOCK TRANSACTION FAILED: Max retries ({max_retries}) reached "
            f"for resources {resource_names}. Possible systemic deadlock."
        )
        return False

    @staticmethod
    def release_multiple(resources: List[LockableResource]):
        """Releases multiple locks in reverse order."""
        # Sorting is not strictly necessary for release but good for consistency
        sorted_resources = sorted(resources, key=lambda r: r.name, reverse=True)
        for res in sorted_resources:
            if res.lock.locked():
                res.lock.release()

# Global Lock Registry to enforce unique names
_LOCK_REGISTRY: Dict[str, RobustLock] = {}

def get_robust_lock(name: str) -> RobustLock:
    """Returns a named RobustLock instance, creating it if necessary."""
    if name not in _LOCK_REGISTRY:
        _LOCK_REGISTRY[name] = RobustLock(name)
    return _LOCK_REGISTRY[name]

class EventLoopMonitor:
    """
    Monitors the asyncio event loop for blocking operations.
    If the loop is delayed by more than 'threshold' seconds beyond its
    intended sleep interval, it logs a warning.
    """
    def __init__(self, threshold: float = 0.1, interval: float = 1.0):
        self.threshold = threshold
        self.interval = interval
        self._stop_event = asyncio.Event()
        self._task: Optional[asyncio.Task] = None
        self._last_lag: float = 0.0

    def start(self):
        """Starts the monitor in a background task."""
        if self._task is not None and not self._task.done():
            return
        self._stop_event.clear()
        self._task = asyncio.create_task(self._run())
        logger.info("🕒 EventLoopMonitor started (threshold=%.2fs, interval=%.1fs)", 
                    self.threshold, self.interval)

    async def stop(self):
        """Stops the monitor gracefully."""
        self._stop_event.set()
        if self._task is not None:
            self._task.cancel()
            try:
                await self._task
            except asyncio.CancelledError:
                pass
        logger.info("🕒 EventLoopMonitor stopped.")

    async def _run(self):
        while not self._stop_event.is_set():
            start_time = time.perf_counter()
            try:
                await asyncio.sleep(self.interval)
            except asyncio.CancelledError:
                break
            
            end_time = time.perf_counter()
            actual_elapsed = end_time - start_time
            lag = actual_elapsed - self.interval

            if lag > self.threshold:
                self._last_lag = lag
                logger.warning(
                    "🚨 EVENT LOOP LAG DETECTED: %.4fs (threshold=%.2fs). "
                    "Something is blocking the event loop!", 
                    lag, self.threshold
                )
